Data TLB contains 256 sets.
Each set contains 4 entries.
Number of bits used for the index is 8.

Number of virtual pages is 8192.
Number of physical pages is 1024.
Each page contains 4096 bytes.
Number of bits used for the page table index is 13.
Number of bits used for the page offset is 12.

D-cache contains 512 sets.
Each set contains 1 entries.
Each line is 16 bytes.
The cache uses a write-allocate and write-back policy.
Number of bits used for the index is 9.
Number of bits used for the offset is 4.

L2-cache contains 2048 sets.
Each set contains 4 entries.
Each line is 16 bytes.
The cache uses a no write-allocate and write-through policy.
Number of bits used for the index is 11.
Number of bits used for the offset is 4.
